29/06/23, 1:24â€¯pm - +91 98302 83416: Dear Students,

We hope this email finds you in good health and high spirits. As we embark on a new academic term, we are thrilled to announce that the IIT Madras BS Film Society is opening its doors to recruit new members who are passionate about the world of films and eager to make a lasting impact in the field.

Our previous projects have garnered acclaim and recognition, including the critically acclaimed and award-nominated documentary film "Breaking Barriers: The IIT Madras Story." We take pride in our ongoing "In Conversation With" series, where we host esteemed guests from the film industry. Some of our esteemed previous guests include Adil Hussain, Dan Mirvish, Ian Simmons, Sumit Purohit, Komal Nahta, and many more.

Now, we are excited to invite you to join our vibrant and creative community as we seek to expand our horizons and continue our journey towards excellence. We have several openings across different teams, offering you a chance to explore your interests and contribute to various aspects of filmmaking and film society management.

PR Team: Join us as a PR Team Member and take charge of promoting and publicizing our society's activities and achievements. Help us create compelling content, organize press conferences, and build strong relationships with media outlets and stakeholders.
Social Media Team: If you have a passion for social media, join our Social Media Team and help us manage our presence on platforms like Instagram, Twitter, YouTube, and LinkedIn. Showcase your creativity by developing engaging content and interacting with our ever-growing online audience.
Sponsorship Team: Become a part of our Sponsorship Team and unlock opportunities to collaborate with businesses and organizations to support our society's initiatives. Build lasting relationships with sponsors and ensure the successful execution of sponsorship agreements.
Design Team: If you have an eye for aesthetics and love creating visually appealing content, our Design Team is the perfect fit for you. Join us in shaping our visual identity through your graphic design skills and contribute to creating captivating marketing materials.
Web Developer: If you have a passion for web development and a keen eye for creating immersive online experiences, our Web Developer position is the perfect fit for you. Join us in shaping the future of our online presence and digital platforms as we leverage technology to enhance the film industry. Collaborate with our talented team to design, develop, and maintain our society's website, ensuring seamless integration and functionality across platforms. 

We believe that by joining the IIT Madras BS Film Society, you will not only enhance your skills and knowledge in filmmaking and the related disciplines but also forge lifelong friendships and connections with fellow film enthusiasts.

If you are interested in joining any of the teams mentioned above, please fill out the application form:

Web Developer : https://forms.gle/cHafsUUmNSToWjpP9
PR and Social Media Team (including Sponsorship Team, Design Team): https://forms.gle/KMGQwu4mbXjfmHor9


Feel free to apply for multiple teams if you have a diverse skill set and are interested in different roles.

We look forward to welcoming you to the IIT Madras BS Film Society and working together to create memorable experiences, impactful projects, and a vibrant film community.
Should you have any questions or require further information, please do not hesitate to reach out to us at film.society@.study.iitm.ac.in

Warm regards,

IIT Madras BS Film Society

The Decorum of the Group Discussion is as follows :
1. A Mediator / Spokesperson will be present who will mediate the disputes and ensure that the discussion is carried away in an effective way.

For this competition, we encourage complete creative freedom! Each director can submit at most two films, and there are no restrictions on the number of actors or the medium of films. Whether you choose to create an animation film, a VR film, or any other format, the choice is yours. The music and other assets used in the film should either be used with permission from the original copyright owner, owned by the filmmakers themselves, or licensed under creative commons.

Judging Criteria:
Your films will be evaluated based on various criteria, including creativity, storytelling, cinematography and editing.We are excited to announce that a panel of experienced judges will be invited to evaluate the submissions and provide valuable feedback.

Award Categories:
The competition will feature multiple award categories, including Best Film, Best Director, Best Cinematography, Best Editing, Best Screenplay, and Audience Choice. Winners in each category will receive well-deserved recognition from the Film Society of IITM BS Degree. Additionally, the selected films will be featured on our YouTube channel and Instagram, granting your work a broader audience and exposure.

Screening and Award Ceremony:
We are thrilled to host a public screening of the shortlisted films, followed by an exciting award ceremony. This event will provide a platform for participants to showcase their talent and celebrate the creative brilliance within our esteemed community.

Submission Deadline and Further Details:
The submission deadline for "Kino Pravda: version 1.0" is 10th August 2023. 

To participate, please visit https://filmfreeway.com/KinoPravada, to register your film and access additional guidelines.

Don't miss this incredible opportunity to share your stories with the world and leave a lasting impact through the magic of filmmaking. We cannot wait to witness the immense talent within our student community.

For any queries or assistance, feel free to reach out to film.society@study.iitm.ac.in
Lights, Camera, Action - Let the creativity begin!

Best regards,
IIT Madras BS Film Society

```As mentioned in the grading document 5 marks will be provided for the Practice Assignments till Week 8. 

Based on practice assignments - 5 marks - applicable to only Foundation & Diploma courses (wherever practice assignments are provided)

If the average of the marks obtained in all the practice assignments (including programming) until week 8 AND mock tests conducted before Quiz 1 & Quiz 2 >= 40/100, students will get 5 marks.

This edition will give talent (especially from India) the opportunity to learn important principles and skills around effective impact and work together on ambitious projects - culminating in a Demo day with prizes of up to $50,000. The program will run from November (2023) to end of March (2024).

Early bird application deadline: September 14th, 23:59 IST.
Final application deadline: October 1st, 23:59 IST.

To learn more, visit https://bit.ly/3PiOVKr
Apply now at http://bit.ly/3KZhsBW

Get to know the Guest:


Ishita Moitra is an exceptional and distinguished screenplay writer who has framed many Bollywood movies and TV series. She is also the screenwriter for the most celebrated series, â€œFour More Shots Please!â€. Her excellent works include, Mere Dad Ki Maruti, Kambakkht Ishq, Half Girlfriend, Maska, Shakuntala Devi and many more. Among her recent works lies, â€˜Rocky aur Rani Ki Prem Kahaniâ€™, directed by Karan Johar, which sent tremors across the box office this year. She has persistently given the best of stories and her screenplays have made the best out of those stories, with most of them being in everybodyâ€™s all time favourite.

Why You Should join:

About the IIT Madras BS Film Society:


For those of you who are new to our community, the IIT Madras BS Film Society is a platform where we celebrate the magic of filmmaking and embrace the diverse stories that cinema has to offer. We host events, workshops, and interviews with industry professionals to expand our understanding of this art form.


For any queries or concerns about the event, please feel free to reach out to us at instagram or email us at film.society@study.iitm.ac.in .



Warm Regards,

IIT Madras BS Film Society

We have given access to the content of the courses which you have registered to in the Sep 2023 term of the IITM BS program in Data Science and Applications. Please follow the steps given below to access the content and submit the assignments before the deadline.

The content will be accessible before the end of today.

Step 1: Open a browser in Incognito mode. Please click the link https://app.onlinedegree.iitm.ac.in/auth/login

Step 2: Log in with your IITM student email id - roll number@ds.study.iitm.ac.in.

Step 3: Go to My Current Courses on the Dashboard

Step 4: Click any of the courses

Step 5: After clicking the course you will be redirected to the course portal called also as Seek portal.

Step 6: In that, you will be able to see the Lectures & Assignments.



Link to grading document:  http://tiny.cc/Sep23_Grading



All the best!

22/09/23, 11:40â€¯pm - +91 98366 91577: We are planning to enable personalised tutoring/mentoring sessions for all the courses of the Foundation and Diploma levels (except English 1 & 2) for the Sept 2023 term

Students who are interested in this personalised tutoring session will be allocated a Senior Student Tutor who willÂ 
Interact with you for about 5 hours every week - discussing the content of the week for that course
Clearing your doubts in content of that week
Assisting with understanding the assignment questions and helping you solve it if you are stuck

The Tutor will be allotted 10 students and as a group - you can fix a mutually convenient time and learn with each other.

Duration: 5 hours/week for 12 weeks of course duration
Live session and support Time: <<Need to update>>
Mode of tutoring: Online
Tutor Allocation: 10 students with 1 tutor

We have seen that this is a very effective way for those students who are unable to study from the program on their own and are unable to clarify their doubts from just the generic live sessions but require more support to go through the course.

What you have to do:

There is payment of Rs. 2000/course for this session which is enabled under the pending payment section. Students who are registered for more than one course have to pay Rs. 2000 for each course before the deadline. Deadline for the payment 25th September 2023. Students who are attending all sessions will get the refund of Rs. 1000 to their student wallet for the respective course.

We hope this email finds you all in good health and high spirits. The IIT Madras BS Film Society, presents to you our next guest for the on-going â€œIn Conversation Withâ€ series, the Magic Creator, the Real Wordsmith who has crafted some of the most iconic films including Rocky aur Rani ki Prem Kahani in recent times, Ishita Moitra.


Get to know the Guest:


Ishita Moitra is an exceptional and distinguished screenplay writer who has framed many Bollywood movies and TV series. She is also the screenwriter for the most celebrated series, â€œFour More Shots Please!â€. Her excellent works include, Mere Dad Ki Maruti, Kambakkht Ishq, Half Girlfriend, Maska, Shakuntala Devi and many more. Among her recent works lies, â€˜Rocky aur Rani Ki Prem Kahaniâ€™, directed by Karan Johar, which sent tremors across the box office this year. She has persistently given the best of stories and her screenplays have made the best out of those stories, with most of them being in everybodyâ€™s all time favourite.

Why You Should join:


Ishita Moitra will be sharing her experiences, discussing the creative process behind writing screenplays, and offering valuable advice to aspiring writers. You will have the opportunity to learn about the innovative approach and the endeavours it takes to build an impactful script and turn it into an amazing cinematic experience. Unveil the backend process of writing a script and unleash the writer that hides within, as she shares her thoughts on storytelling, challenges faced in the film industry, her vision for the future scripts and her ability to connect with audiences worldwide and excel in all genres, be it a comedy like Mere Dad Ki Maruti or a legend like Shakuntala Devi.

Looking forward to your enthusiastic participation!



About the IIT Madras BS Film Society:


For those of you who are new to our community, the IIT Madras BS Film Society is a platform where we celebrate the magic of filmmaking and embrace the diverse stories that cinema has to offer. We host events, workshops, and interviews with industry professionals to expand our understanding of this art form.


For any queries or concerns about the event, please feel free to reach out to us at instagram or email us at film.society@study.iitm.ac.in .
